// 0=Aries(odd),1=Taurus(even)... if (isOdd) return inSign < 15 ? 4 : 3; // Leo=4, Cancer=3 else return inSign < 15 ? 3 : 4; } // ── D3 Drekkana — Method 1: Parasara "Same → 5th → 9th" rule // 0°–10° → same sign (k=0: +0) // 10°–20° → 5th sign (k=1: +4 signs, i.e. 4 steps from same sign = 5th sign) // 20°–30° → 9th sign (k=2: +8 signs, i.e. 8 steps from same sign = 9th sign) function getDrekkanaParasaraRasi(sidDeg) { var ri = Math.floor(sidDeg / 30) % 12; var k = Math.floor((sidDeg % 30) / 10); // 0,1,2 return (ri + k * 4) % 12; } // ── D3 Drekkana — Method 2: Jaimini Element/Trine method // Fire signs (Ar=0, Le=4, Sa=8) → trine order: 0→0, 1→4, 2→8 // Earth signs (Ta=1, Vi=5, Cp=9) → trine order: 0→1, 1→5, 2→9 // Air signs (Ge=2, Li=6, Aq=10) → trine order: 0→2, 1→6, 2→10 // Water signs (Cn=3, Sc=7, Pi=11) → trine order: 0→3, 1→7, 2→11 // In all cases: result = (element_base + k*4) % 12 // element_base = ri % 4 (0=fire,1=earth,2=air,3=water) // Note: gives identical result to Parasara method ✓ function getDrekkanaJaiminiRasi(sidDeg) { var ri = Math.floor(sidDeg / 30) % 12; var k = Math.floor((sidDeg % 30) / 10); // 0,1,2 var base = ri % 4; // element base: 0=Ar,1=Ta,2=Ge,3=Cn return (base + k * 4) % 12; } // Default D3 uses Parasara method function getDrekkanaRasi(sidDeg) { return getDrekkanaParasaraRasi(sidDeg); } // ── D9 Navamsa — THE CORRECT Parasara formula // Each sign has 9 navamsas of 3°20' each. // Start sign for each rasi (NAV_START): // Fire signs (Ar,Le,Sa = 0,4,8) → start from Aries(0) // Earth signs(Ta,Vi,Cp = 1,5,9) → start from Capricorn(9) // Air signs (Ge,Li,Aq = 2,6,10) → start from Libra(6) // Water signs(Cn,Sc,Pi = 3,7,11) → start from Cancer(3) var D9_START = [0,9,6,3, 0,9,6,3, 0,9,6,3]; function getNavamsaRasiCorrect(sidDeg) { var ri = Math.floor(sidDeg / 30) % 12; var inSign = sidDeg % 30; var seg = Math.min(Math.floor(inSign / (30/9)), 8); // 0-8 return (D9_START[ri] + seg) % 12; } // ── D12 Dwadasamsa — starts from sign itself, both odd and even function getDwadasamsaRasi(sidDeg) { var ri = Math.floor(sidDeg / 30) % 12; var part = Math.min(Math.floor((sidDeg % 30) / 2.5), 11); return (ri + part) % 12; } // ── D60 Shashtiamsa — 60 parts of 0.5° each // Odd signs: start from Aries(0); Even signs: start from sign itself function getShashtiamsaRasi(sidDeg) { var ri = Math.floor(sidDeg / 30) % 12; var part = Math.min(Math.floor((sidDeg % 30) / 0.5), 59); var start = (ri % 2 === 0) ? 0 : ri; return (start + part) % 12; } // ── Generic varga (D4,5,6,7,8,10,11,16,20,24,27,30,40,45) // oddStart = where part-0 maps to for odd signs // evenStart = where part-0 maps to for even signs (null = sign itself) function getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, N, oddStart, evenStart) { var ri = Math.floor(sidDeg / 30) % 12; var part = Math.min(Math.floor((sidDeg % 30) / (30/N)), N-1); var isOdd = ri % 2 === 0; var start = isOdd ? oddStart : (evenStart === null ? ri : evenStart); return (start + part) % 12; } // ── Master dispatcher — all correct Parasara rules function calcVargaForDeg(sidDeg, d) { switch(d) { case 1: return Math.floor(sidDeg / 30) % 12; case 2: return getHoraRasi(sidDeg); case 3: return getDrekkanaRasi(sidDeg); case 4: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 4, 0, 3); // odd→Ar, even→Ca case 5: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 5, 0, 4); // odd→Ar, even→Le case 6: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 6, 0, 8); // odd→Ar, even→Sa case 7: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 7, 0, 6); // odd→Ar, even→Li case 8: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 8, 0, 9); // odd→Ar, even→Cp case 9: return getNavamsaRasiCorrect(sidDeg); // Parasara NAV_START case 10: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 10, 0, 4); // odd→Ar, even→Le case 11: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 11, 0, 8); // odd→Ar, even→Sa case 12: return getDwadasamsaRasi(sidDeg); // starts from sign case 16: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 16, 0, 6); // odd→Ar, even→Li case 20: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 20, 0, 8); // odd→Ar, even→Sa case 24: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 24, 0, 4); // odd→Ar, even→Le case 27: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 27, 0, 4); // odd→Ar, even→Le case 30: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 30, 0, 6); // odd→Ar, even→Li case 40: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 40, 0, 6); // odd→Ar, even→Li case 45: return getGenericVargaRasi(sidDeg, 45, 0, 4); // odd→Ar, even→Le case 60: return getShashtiamsaRasi(sidDeg); default: return Math.floor(sidDeg / 30) % 12; } } // ── Also fix getNavamsaRasi (used in gochara) to use same correct formula function getNavamsaRasi(sidDeg) { return getNavamsaRasiCorrect(sidDeg); } // ── Calculate all 20 vargas function calcShodashavarga(birthData) { var positions = birthData.positions; var lagna = birthData.lagna; var mandi = birthData.mandi || null; var result = {}; VARGA_INFO.forEach(function(vi) { var d = vi.d; var lagRi = calcVargaForDeg(lagna.sidDeg, d); var planRis = positions.slice(0, 9).map(function(p) { return calcVargaForDeg(p.sidDeg, d); }); var mandiRi = mandi ? calcVargaForDeg(mandi.sidDeg, d) : -1; result[d] = { lagRi:lagRi, planRis:planRis, mandiRi:mandiRi }; }); // D3 Jaimini (element/trine method) — stored separately result["3j"] = { lagRi: getDrekkanaJaiminiRasi(lagna.sidDeg), planRis: positions.slice(0, 9).map(function(p) { return getDrekkanaJaiminiRasi(p.sidDeg); }), mandiRi: mandi ? getDrekkanaJaiminiRasi(mandi.sidDeg) : -1 }; // ── Jaimini Chara Karaka (7 karakas, excluding Rahu & Ketu from ranking) // Rule: rank Sun,Moon,Mars,Mercury,Jupiter,Venus,Saturn by degree-within-sign descending // Rahu/Ketu special rule: // If Rahu has highest degree-in-sign among planets → Rahu's sign lord gets AK rank // If Ketu has highest degree-in-sign among planets → Rahu (not Ketu) gets the rank // The 7 karakas in order: AK, AmK, BK, MK, PK, GK, DK var KARAKA_NAMES_EN = ["Atmakaraka","Amatyakaraka","Bhratrukaraka","Matrukaraka","Putrakaraka","Gnatikaraka","Darakaraka"]; var KARAKA_NAMES_TA = ["ஆத்மகாரகன்","அமாத்யகாரகன்","பிரத்ருகாரகன்","மாத்ருகாரகன்","புத்ரகாரகன்","ஞாதிகாரகன்","தாரகாரகன்"]; var KARAKA_SHORT_EN = ["AK","AmK","BK","MK","PK","GK","DK"]; var KARAKA_MEANING_EN = ["Soul significator","Career / Minister","Siblings","Mother","Children","Enemies / Obstacles","Spouse"]; var KARAKA_MEANING_TA = ["ஆன்மா காரகன்","தொழில் / அமைச்சர்","உடன்பிறப்பு","தாய்","பிள்ளைகள்","எதிரிகள் / தடைகள்","வாழ்க்கைத்துணை"]; // Planets 0-6 = Sun,Moon,Mars,Mercury,Jupiter,Venus,Saturn (exclude Rahu=7, Ketu=8) // Jaimini rule: retrograde planets count degree from END of sign (30 - deg_in_sign) var karakaPool = []; // { pl, inSign } positions.slice(0, 7).forEach(function(p, i) { var raw = p.sidDeg % 30; var inSign = p.retro ? (30 - raw) : raw; karakaPool.push({ pl:i, inSign: inSign, retro: !!p.retro }); }); // Check Rahu(7) and Ketu(8) — Rahu/Ketu are always retrograde by nature // For Jaimini: Rahu inSign uses (30 - raw) since Rahu is always retrograde var rahuRaw = positions[7] ? positions[7].sidDeg % 30 : 0; var ketuRaw = positions[8] ? positions[8].sidDeg % 30 : 0; var rahuInSign = 30 - rahuRaw; // Rahu always retrograde var ketuInSign = 30 - ketuRaw; // Ketu always retrograde // Rahu/Ketu can compete for AK only — if their in-sign degree beats all 7 planets, // Rahu (or Rahu as stand-in for Ketu) takes AK and pushes others down var maxPlanetDeg = karakaPool.reduce(function(mx, k){ return k.inSign > mx ? k.inSign : mx; }, 0); var rahuIsAK = false, rahuWasByKetu = false; if (rahuInSign > maxPlanetDeg) { rahuIsAK = true; } else if (ketuInSign > maxPlanetDeg) { rahuIsAK = true; rahuWasByKetu = true; } // Sort pool descending by inSign karakaPool.sort(function(a,b){ return b.inSign - a.inSign; }); // Assign karakas var karakas = []; if (rahuIsAK) { // Rahu takes slot 0 (AK), planets fill slots 1-6 (AmK..DK) karakas.push({ pl:7, inSign: rahuIsAK && !rahuWasByKetu ? rahuInSign : ketuInSign, actualPl: rahuWasByKetu ? 8 : 7, byKetu: rahuWasByKetu }); karakaPool.slice(0, 6).forEach(function(k){ karakas.push(k); }); } else { karakaPool.slice(0, 7).forEach(function(k){ karakas.push(k); }); } result.karakas = karakas; // array of 7: [{pl, inSign}, ...] pl=0-8 result.atmakaraka = karakas[0].pl; // planet index of AK (may be 7=Rahu) result.akDegInSign = karakas[0].inSign; result.rahuIsAK = rahuIsAK; result.rahuWasByKetu = rahuWasByKetu; result.karakamsa = result[9] ? result[9].planRis[Math.min(result.atmakaraka, 8)] : null; return result; } // ── Jaimini Chara Karaka Table — shared by Gochara and Shodashavarga function CharaKarakaTable(props) { var vd = props.vd; // result of calcShodashavarga or similar var pos = props.positions; // raw positions array from birthData/gocharaData var isTA = props.isTA; if (!vd || !vd.karakas || !pos) return null; var pN = function(i){ return isTA ? PL_TA[i] : PL_EN[i]; }; var sh = function(i){ return isTA ? PL_STA[i] : PL_SEN[i]; }; var KARAKA_NAMES_EN = ["Atmakaraka","Amatyakaraka","Bhratrukaraka","Matrukaraka","Putrakaraka","Gnatikaraka","Darakaraka"]; var KARAKA_NAMES_TA = ["ஆத்மகாரகன்","அமாத்யகாரகன்","பிரத்ருகாரகன்","மாத்ருகாரகன்","புத்ரகாரகன்","ஞாதிகாரகன்","தாரகாரகன்"]; var KARAKA_SHORT = ["AK","AmK","BK","MK","PK","GK","DK"]; var KARAKA_MEANING_EN = ["Soul significator","Career / Minister","Siblings","Mother","Children","Enemies / Obstacles","Spouse"]; var KARAKA_MEANING_TA = ["ஆன்மா காரகன்","தொழில் / அமைச்சர்","உடன்பிறப்பு","தாய்","பிள்ளைகள்","எதிரிகள் / தடைகள்","வாழ்க்கைத்துணை"]; var SLOT_CLR = [C.acc2,"#cc88ff","#44cc88","#ff9955","#55ddff","#ff5577","#88aaff"]; var hdS = { background:C.bg3, color:C.acc, padding:"6px 8px", textAlign:"left", fontSize:"10px", textTransform:"uppercase", borderBottom:"1px solid "+C.bdr, whiteSpace:"nowrap" }; // Special note about Rahu/Ketu var rahuNote = null; if (vd.rahuIsAK) { rahuNote = ce("div",{style:{background:C.warnBg,border:"1px solid "+C.acc,borderRadius:"6px", padding:"7px 12px",marginBottom:"10px",fontSize:"11px",color:C.acc2,lineHeight:1.7}}, vd.rahuWasByKetu ? (isTA ? "⚠ கேது அதிக பாகை பெற்றதால் — விதிப்படி ராகு ஆத்மகாரகனாக ஆகிறான் (கேது → ராகு விதி)" : "⚠ Ketu has highest degree-in-sign — by rule, Rahu becomes Atmakaraka on Ketu's behalf") : (isTA ? "⚠ ராகு அதிக பாகை பெற்று ஆத்மகாரகனாக ஆகிறான்" : "⚠ Rahu has highest degree-in-sign and becomes Atmakaraka") ); } return ce("div",{style:{background:C.bg2,border:"1px solid "+C.bdr,borderRadius:"9px", padding:"14px",marginTop:"14px"}}, ce("div",{style:{color:C.acc,fontWeight:700,fontSize:"12px",letterSpacing:"1px", textTransform:"uppercase",marginBottom:"10px",paddingBottom:"6px",borderBottom:"1px solid "+C.bdrGold}}, isTA?"ஜைமினி சர காரக அட்டவணை":"Jaimini Chara Karaka Table"), rahuNote, ce("div",{style:{overflowX:"auto"}}, ce("table",{style:{width:"100%",borderCollapse:"collapse",fontSize:"12px"}}, ce("thead",null, ce("tr",null, ce("th",{style:Object.assign({},hdS,{width:"28px",textAlign:"center"})}, "#"), ce("th",{style:hdS}, isTA?"காரகன்":"Karaka"), ce("th",{style:hdS}, isTA?"கிரகம்":"Planet"), ce("th",{style:{background:C.bg3,color:"#7799ff",padding:"6px 8px", fontSize:"10px",textTransform:"uppercase",borderBottom:"1px solid "+C.bdr,whiteSpace:"nowrap"}}, isTA?"பாகை (ராசியில்)":"Degree in Sign"), ce("th",{style:hdS}, isTA?"பொருள்":"Meaning") ) ), ce("tbody",null, vd.karakas.map(function(k, idx) { var bg = idx%2===0?C.bg2:C.bg4; var tdS = {padding:"7px 8px",background:bg,borderBottom:"1px solid "+C.bdr}; var clr = SLOT_CLR[idx]; var plIdx = k.pl; var isRahu = plIdx === 7; var isKetu = plIdx === 8; var plLabel = isRahu ? (isTA?"ராகு":"Rahu") : isKetu ? (isTA?"கேது":"Ketu") : pN(plIdx); var plShort = isRahu ? (isTA?"ரா":"Ra") : isKetu ? (isTA?"கே":"Ke") : sh(plIdx); var deg = k.inSign; var kName = isTA ? KARAKA_NAMES_TA[idx] : KARAKA_NAMES_EN[idx]; var kMean = isTA ? KARAKA_MEANING_TA[idx] : KARAKA_MEANING_EN[idx]; return ce("tr",{key:idx}, ce("td",{style:Object.assign({},tdS,{textAlign:"center"})}, ce("span",{style:{color:clr,fontWeight:800,fontFamily:"monospace",fontSize:"13px"}}, idx+1)), ce("td",{style:tdS}, ce("div",{style:{color:clr,fontWeight:700,fontSize:"11px"}}, KARAKA_SHORT[idx]), ce("div",{style:{color:C.muted2,fontSize:"10px",marginTop:"1px"}}, kName) ), ce("td",{style:tdS}, ce("span",{style:{color:plClr(Math.min(plIdx,11)),fontWeight:700,fontFamily:"monospace",fontSize:"13px"}}, plShort), ce("span",{style:{color:C.muted2,fontSize:"10px",marginLeft:"5px"}}, plLabel), isRahu && k.byKetu && ce("span",{style:{color:C.muted,fontSize:"9px",marginLeft:"4px"}},"(via Ke)") ), ce("td",{style:Object.assign({},tdS,{fontFamily:"monospace",color:C.acc2,fontSize:"12px"})}, deg.toFixed(2)+"°"), ce("td",{style:Object.assign({},tdS,{color:C.muted2,fontSize:"11px"})}, kMean) ); }) ) ) ) ); } // ── Single Varga Chart (South Indian, compact) // ── VargaAnalysisBox — Trikona/Kendra, Nakshatra Saram, Vayathottam, Multi-aspect ────── function VargaAnalysisBox(props) { useTheme(); var birthData = props.birthData; var lagRi = props.lagRi; // varga lagna rasi var planRis = props.planRis; // planet varga rasis [0..8] var isTA = props.isTA; var viName = props.viName || "D1"; var isD1 = props.isD1 === true; var age = props.age; // optional: for vayathottam var pN = function(i){ return isTA ? PL_TA[i] : PL_EN[i]; }; var rN = function(i){ return isTA ? RS_TA[i] : RS_EN[i]; }; var nkN = function(i){ return isTA ? NK[i][0] : NK[i][1]; }; function rasiToHouse(ri) { return ((ri - lagRi + 12) % 12) + 1; } function houseLord(h) { return RS_LORD[(lagRi + h - 1) % 12]; } var positions = birthData.positions || []; var d1LagRi = birthData.lagna.ri; function d1House(ri) { return ((ri - d1LagRi + 12) % 12) + 1; } // ── 1. Trikona / Kendra grouping ────────────────────────────── var TRIKONA = [1,5,9], KENDRA = [4,7,10], UPACHAYA = [3,6,11], DHANA = [2,8,12]; function houseGroup(h) { if (TRIKONA.indexOf(h) !== -1) return { label:isTA?"திரிகோணம்":"Trikona", color:"#44ff88", abbr:"T" }; if (KENDRA.indexOf(h) !== -1) return { label:isTA?"கேந்திரம்":"Kendra", color:"#55ddff", abbr:"K" }; if (UPACHAYA.indexOf(h)!== -1) return { label:isTA?"உபசயம்":"Upachaya", color:"#ffaa44", abbr:"U" }; return { label:isTA?"தன ஸ்தானம்":"Dhana", color:"#cc88ff", abbr:"D" }; } var trikonaPlans = [], kendraPlans = [], otherPlans = []; planRis.forEach(function(vRi, i) { var h = rasiToHouse(vRi); var g = houseGroup(h); var entry = { pl:i, name:pN(i), color:plClr(i), house:h, group:g }; if (TRIKONA.indexOf(h) !== -1) trikonaPlans.push(entry); else if (KENDRA.indexOf(h) !== -1) kendraPlans.push(entry); else otherPlans.push(entry); }); // Lagna var lagH = rasiToHouse(lagRi); var lagG = houseGroup(lagH); // ── 2. Nakshatra Saram ───────────────────────────────────────── // For each planet: which house does its star lord occupy? // That star lord house reveals the "saram" (essence) of the planet var nkSaram = planRis.map(function(vRi, i) { var p = positions[i]; if (!p) return null; var nl = p.nl; // star lord planet index var nlPos = positions[nl]; if (!nlPos) return null; var nlVRi = planRis[nl]; // star lord varga rasi var nlH = rasiToHouse(nlVRi !== undefined ? nlVRi : nlPos.ri); var nlG = houseGroup(nlH); return { pl:i, name:pN(i), color:plClr(i), nlPl:nl, nlName:pN(nl), nlColor:plClr(nl), nlHouse:nlH, nlGroup:nlG, nkName: nkN(p.ni), pada: Math.min(Math.floor(((p.sidDeg*60)-(p.ni*800))/200)+1,4) }; }).filter(Boolean); // ── 3. Vayathottam (Age Progression) ────────────────────────── // Each house = a life period. 1-12, then 13-24, etc. // Current age house = (age-1) % 12 + 1 var vayaH = age ? ((parseInt(age)-1) % 12 + 1) : null; var vayaRi = vayaH ? (lagRi + vayaH - 1) % 12 : null; var vayaPlanets = vayaH ? planRis.map(function(ri,i){ return ri === vayaRi ? { pl:i, name:pN(i), color:plClr(i) } : null; }).filter(Boolean) : []; // House lord of current vaya house var vayaLord = vayaH ? houseLord(vayaH) : null; // Marriage trigger houses: 1,3,5,7,11 var MARRIAGE_H = [1,3,5,7,11]; var isMarriageVaya = vayaH && MARRIAGE_H.indexOf(vayaH) !== -1; // ── 4. Multi-aspect convergence ─────────────────────────────── // Standard aspects: all planets aspect 7th. Mars:4,7,8. Jupiter:5,7,9. Saturn:3,7,10. Rahu/Ketu:5,7,9 function getAspectHouses(pl, fromH) { var base = [((fromH+6-1)%12)+1]; // 7th from planet if (pl === 2) base.push(((fromH+3-1)%12)+1, ((fromH+7-1)%12)+1); // Mars: +4,+8 if (pl === 4) base.push(((fromH+4-1)%12)+1, ((fromH+8-1)%12)+1); // Jupiter: +5,+9 if (pl === 6) base.push(((fromH+2-1)%12)+1, ((fromH+9-1)%12)+1); // Saturn: +3,+10 if (pl === 7 || pl === 8) base.push(((fromH+4-1)%12)+1, ((fromH+8-1)%12)+1); // Rahu/Ketu return Array.from(new Set(base)); } // Count how many planets aspect each house var aspectCount = {}; for (var h=1;h<=12;h++) aspectCount[h]=[]; planRis.forEach(function(vRi, i) { var fromH = rasiToHouse(vRi); getAspectHouses(i, fromH).forEach(function(ah) { if (!aspectCount[ah]) aspectCount[ah]=[]; aspectCount[ah].push(i); }); }); // Houses with 3+ aspects = convergence var convergence = []; for (var hh=1;hh<=12;hh++) { if (aspectCount[hh] && aspectCount[hh].length >= 3) { convergence.push({ house:hh, planets:aspectCount[hh] }); } } convergence.sort(function(a,b){ return b.planets.length - a.planets.length; }); var _tab = React.useState("lagpathi"), activeTab = _tab[0], setActiveTab = _tab[1]; var _age = React.useState(""), ageInp = _age[0], setAgeInp = _age[1]; // ── Lagnathipathi analysis ────────────────────────────────── var lagLord = RS_LORD[d1LagRi]; // Lagnathipathi planet var lagLordPos = positions[lagLord]; // D1 position var lagLordVRi = planRis[lagLord]; // Varga rasi of Lagnathipathi var lagLordH = lagLordVRi !== undefined ? rasiToHouse(lagLordVRi) : null; var lagLordG = lagLordH ? houseGroup(lagLordH) : null; // Star lord of Lagnathipathi var lagLordNl = lagLordPos ? lagLordPos.nl : null; var lagLordNlPos = lagLordNl !== null && lagLordNl !== undefined ? positions[lagLordNl] : null; var lagLordNlVRi = lagLordNl !== null && lagLordNl !== undefined ? planRis[lagLordNl] : null; var lagLordNlH = lagLordNlVRi !== undefined ? rasiToHouse(lagLordNlVRi) : null; var lagLordNlG = lagLordNlH ? houseGroup(lagLordNlH) : null; var lagLordNk = lagLordPos ? nkN(lagLordPos.ni) : "-"; var lagLordPada = lagLordPos ? Math.min(Math.floor(((lagLordPos.sidDeg*60)-(lagLordPos.ni*800))/200)+1,4) : null; // Sub lord of Lagnathipathi var lagLordSubl = lagLordPos ? lagLordPos.subl : null; var lagLordSublVRi = lagLordSubl !== null && lagLordSubl !== undefined ? planRis[lagLordSubl] : null; var lagLordSublH = lagLordSublVRi !== undefined ? rasiToHouse(lagLordSublVRi) : null; var lagLordSublG = lagLordSublH ? houseGroup(lagLordSublH) : null; var tabs = [ { id:"lagpathi", label:isTA?"லக்னாதிபதி":"Lagnathipathi" }, { id:"trikona", label:isTA?"திரிகோணம்/கேந்திரம்":"Trikona/Kendra" }, isD1 && { id:"saram", label:isTA?"நட்சத்திர சாரம்":"Nakshatra Saram" }, isD1 && { id:"vaya", label:isTA?"வயோத்தோட்டம்":"Vayathottam" }, { id:"aspect", label:isTA?"பல கிரக பார்வை":"Multi-Aspect" } ].filter(Boolean); var tabBtnStyle = function(id) { return { padding:"5px 12px", fontSize:"10px", fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", border:"none", borderBottom: activeTab===id ? "2px solid "+C.acc : "2px solid transparent", background:"transparent", color: activeTab===id ? C.acc2 : C.muted, letterSpacing:"0.3px" }; }; return ce("div",{style:{marginTop:"14px",background:C.bg4,border:"1px solid "+C.bdr, borderRadius:"10px",overflow:"hidden"}}, // Tab strip ce("div",{style:{display:"flex",borderBottom:"1px solid "+C.bdr,background:C.bg3, overflowX:"auto",scrollbarWidth:"none"}}, tabs.map(function(t){ return
